Even after people acknowledge their bias or strong belief, the discourse gravitates towards proving why your belief is better than the others. It rarely stops at trying to understand the other side’s perspective or respecting the other sides POV. ↵ More often than not, there is a lack of context which prevents a total understanding. So our views are shaped by the news / views we consume that aligns with our nascent beliefs. ↵ Having said that, I do love getting engaged in such a discourse but I lack a total understanding / context of the politics at times to put forward a compelling case.

[2026-01-25T22:47:28Z] Pavan Pamidimarri: Q.	Central banks issuing banknotes must ensure that they keep meticulous track of how many notes are printed, so that they can control money supply in the economy, a key tool in monetary policy. Modern high-speed printing presses used to manufacture currency notes in the United States and India require serial numbers to be in a strict mathematical sequence. When Quality Control inspects each sheet for errors; if any errors are found, the entire sheet is discarded. Stopping the press to reprint notes with those same serial numbers as the discarded ones would be very inefficient. Instead, a pre-printed sheet with different serial numbers and a X next to the serial number is inserted in place of the discarded sheet. Because printing errors are rare, notes with a X sign on them are rare, which make them attractive to collectors, increasing their value. Collectors call them “X notes.” ID X.

A wind rose is a diagram used by meteorologists to give a succinct view of how wind speed and direction are typically distributed at a particular location. Wind roses were predecessors of the compass rose, found on nautical charts. Using a polar coordinate system of gridding, the frequency of winds over a time period is plotted by wind direction, with colour bands showing wind speed ranges. The direction of the longest spoke shows the wind direction with the greatest frequency, the prevailing wind. Wind roses are essential when making the most important decisions about X design. [2026-01-26T04:30:53Z] Pavan Pamidimarri: 1.	When Cyril Radcliffe partitioned a country he had no prior knowledge about in unseemly haste, he and his team made mistakes. One such mistake was the Berubari Union No. 12 in the Jalpaiguri district of West Bengal. The Radcliffe documents were contradictory; the intent was for that land to be part of India, but some maps showed them in East Pakistan. After negotiations, India and Pakistan agreed to split the territory halfway. Faced with fierce opposition in West Bengal, the President asked the Supreme Court for an advisory opinion. In the famous case “In Re: The Berubari Union” the court ruled in 1960 that a constitutional amendment is necessary to cede territory to another country. It also said that X serves as a key to understanding the minds of the makers of the Constitution, but X is not part of the Constitution itself. ID X.

Because of its vast size and scope, it has been nicknamed the “X Y.” In addition to changing the Preamble, this amendment sought to push the system towards parliamentary sovereignty and remove checks on legislative power: the President as the head of the executive branch must follow the advise of the Cabinet elected by the legislature, and the courts could no longer check the legislature’s powers to enact laws and amendments.
